 The history of Moradabad Lok Sabha seat, also known as Brass Nagari, continues since 1952
 yahaan par pehali baar 1952 main loksabhaa chunaav hue
 Congress won from here twice in a row
 1967 or 1971 main ye seat bhartiya jansangh ke khate main gai
 Chaudhary Charan Singh's party, Bharatiya Lok Dal, won the 1977 Lok Sabha election after the Emergency
 1980 main ek baar phir janata dal ne yahaan se jeet hasil kii, lekin 1984 main desh main chali congress kii lahar main seat phir congress ke khate main gai
 Then in 1989 and 1991, this Lok Sabha seat went to Janata Dal account, in 1996 and 1998 to Samajwadi Party
 congress se tuutakar bani jagdambika paal kii akhil bhartiya loktantric congress ne 1999 chunaav main is seat se jeet darj kii thi

 In such a situation, the Indian cricket team would like to start the journey of victory in the 'auspicious time', leaving behind their bad phase while playing with England on Tuesday
 bhartiya team paanch maichon kii ekadivasiy shrunkhlaa main 0-1 se peeche chal rahi he
 Only time will tell whether she will be able to make a fresh start with a win in Kochi, but the last one month has been very bad for India
 use england ke haathon test shrunkhlaa main haar mili or phir pakistan ke haathon ekadivasiy shrunkhlaa ganvaani padi
 In Rajkot, India had scored 316 runs chasing a mammoth target of 326 runs
 vah match kai lihaaj se ahm tha

 He has to manage himself before the home Test series with Australia and for that he will have to win over the English team

 The absence of the in-form Cheteshwar Pujara in the playing XI had caused criticism for Dhoni
 dhoni rabindra jadeja ke sthaan par pujaara ko team main shaamil kar sakate the lekin beete match main pakistan ke khilaaf harfanmaulaa pradarshan karne vaale jadeja ko captain kaa bharosa mila or is tarah bharat ko ek achche farm main chal rahe ballebaaj ke bina hi maidan main utarana padaa
 This time is bad for Dhoni
 ek samay tha, jab vah jis cheez ko choote the, sona ho jaataa tha lekin aaj halaat badal chuke hai
 There was a time when Dhoni's wrong decisions were also proved correct, but today many of his right decisions are also proved wrong

 This is more important for the team because without Sachin Tendulkar and Virender Sehwag, the team is seen to be weak anyway
 or to or salaami ballebaaj beete saal se lekar ab tak ek maukey par bhi acchhee shuruyaat nahin de sake hai
 The team lacks balance of performance
 yahi kaaran he jab gendbaaj acha karte hai to ballebaaj flop ho jate hai or jab ballebaaj chamakate hai to gendbaaj kaam kharaab kar dete hai
 In Rajkot, three England batsmen had scored more than 100 runs and four batsmen of India were able to make more than this average but despite this the team lost
 kaaran saaf he, bhartiya ballebaajon ko kuch or der tak wicket par tike rahanaa hoga

 duusari ore, english team ke saamne bharat se kaaphi kam chintaaen hai
 His batsmen are in good rhythm and the bowlers are doing their job well

 do abhyaas maichon se lekar ab tak bel ek shatak or do ardhshtak laga chuke hai

 They have all proved this in Rajkot

 dhoni ke liye yah vakt kharaab he
 There was a time when everything he used to touch would become gold, but today things have changed

 In such a situation, Dhoni should intentionally inspire his teammates to play well while avoiding any stubbornness or mistake
 yah team ke liye zyada jaruri he kyonki sachin tendulkar or virendra sahvaag ke bagaiyr team vaise bhi kamjor padati dikhaai de rahi he

 team main pradarshan ke santulan kaa abhaav he

 The reason is simple, Indian batsmen will have to stay on the wicket for some more time

 ) The country's Supreme Court has given a major decision on electoral bonds on Friday
 ab sabhi raajnneetik dalon ko elactoral bond dene vaale daataaon ke naam chunaav ayog ko dene honge
 The Central Government had demanded that the matter be deferred till the completion of the Lok Sabha elections
 lekin, supreme court ne is maamle par faisla sunaaya
 Understand what the court's verdict is and what can happen next
 
 
 1
 The Supreme Court has shown strictness regarding electoral bonds
 ab sabhi raajnneetik dalon ko 30 may tak silband lipaphe main bond ke jariye milane vaale chande kii jaankaree deni hogi
 2
 matlab ye he ki 15 may tak mili rakam kaa sabhi dalon ko hisaab bataanaa hoga or un logon ke khaaton kii bhi jaankaree deni hogi jahaan se ye bond in dalon ko mili hai
 3
 centre sarkaar ne chunavi chande main paardarshita laane ke naam par ek hajaar-das hajaar-ek lakh-das lakh tak ke chunavi band jari kiye the
 Any citizen could buy these bonds and donate to the parties in a way
 4
 Earlier the condition was that the names of the bond purchasers were to be kept confidential but today the Supreme Court has also asked for the names of the donors
 or inhen chunaav ayog ko dene kii jaankaree di he
 5
 bond kharidne waalon ko apane balance shit main raajnneetik dal ke kharide gaye bond kaa zikr karnaa hoga
 6
 in chunavi bond ko bharat kaa koi bhi naagarik un dalon ko de saktaa he, jinhen pichley chunaavon main kul voton kaa kam se kam ek fisadi vot mila tha
 7
 sarkaar ne bond kharidne ke liye pehle 55 dinon kaa samay rakhaa tha, is dauraan janvari, april, july or oktober main bond kharide jate the
 Earlier this time was 50 days but later it was extended to 5 days
 8
 The Supreme Court has also reversed this decision, now only 50 days the bond can be used
 9
 According to the ADR report, Rs 222 crore was donated by electoral bonds in 2017-18
 10
 210 crores (94) to BJP
 5%), congress ko 5 karod rupye or baaki dalon ko 7 karod rupye hasil hue hai

 mohammad ajaharuddin ne england main shrinkhalaa haarane ke baad 1996 main jab captaini ganvaai thi to sachin tendulkar team kii kaman sanbhaalane ke liye taiyaar the or kisi ne unhen yah bhoomika saunpane par sawaal bhi nahin uthaaya

 Ricky Ponting was given the one-day captaincy following the team's defeat in the 2011 World Cup, while the team he led had won the last two World Cups
 ponting ko isse pehle varsh 2000 main steve vaa kii jagah captain banaaya gaya tha jinhone australia ko sheersh par pahunchane main ahm bhoomika nibhaai thi
 Viv Richards earned no series as captain and led the team to win 27 of 50 Tests, but was forced to retire despite Richie Richardson being given command of the team
 pakistan main captainon ko unke pad se hataaya janaa badi baat nahin he

 in is presenting a series on similar incidents of sex scandal
 is kadi main aaj pesh he haryana ke purv mantri gopal kanda kii kahani
 a person who earns a few hundred rupees a month by doing bad radio repair, when he starts selling shoes and then after selling shoes, takes the feet of the leaders and puts his feet in the airplane, it is not known
 nazren aasmaan main thim or nigahen hawaii jahaaj par
 It was the early nineties
 haryana ke chote se shahar sirsa main tab gopal goyal kanda kii radio repere kii ek choti si dukaan thi
 Jupiter Music Home
 is dukaan se maheene main bamushkil kuch sau rupee kii hi aamadani hoti thi
 But by now Kanda's eyes had fallen on the plane in the sky
 use pataa tha ki radio repere karne kii ek maamuli si dukaan se wo aasmaan tak kaa safai tay nahin kar saktaa tha
 So, without delay, Kanda locked up his Jupiter music home and started a new business in association with his brother Govind Kanda
 is baar usne juute or chappal kii dukaan kholi, kanda shu camp
 The shop went on and then the two brothers started a shoe-making factory, increasing their business
 ab donon khud juuta banaate or apni dukaan main bechate
 By selling shoes, Kanda had measured the feet of many businessmen, builders, brokers and politicians
 raajnneeti ko bananaa chahta tha kaarobaarrajnneetik talvon ko naapane kii shuruuaat kanda ne bansilaal ke bete se kii
